+CREATE TABLE notification_preferences (
+    user_id                       UUID PRIMARY KEY REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
+    assistance_requests_enabled   BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT TRUE,
+    push_enabled                  BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT TRUE,
+    created_at                    TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
+    updated_at                    TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
+);
+
+CREATE TRIGGER update_notification_preferences_updated_at
+    BEFORE UPDATE ON notification_preferences
+    FOR EACH ROW
+    EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();
+
+-- Assistance-request notifications should be inserted in the same transaction
+-- as the device status transition and device_events row so the alert cannot be
+-- lost if part of the workflow fails.
+CREATE TABLE notifications (
+    id              UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
+    user_id         UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
+    device_id       UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES devices(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
+    device_event_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES device_events(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
+    kind            VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
+    title           TEXT NOT NULL,
+    body            TEXT NOT NULL,
+    read            BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT FALSE,
+    created_at      TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
+    updated_at      TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
+    CONSTRAINT notifications_user_event_unique UNIQUE (user_id, device_event_id)
+);
+
+CREATE INDEX idx_notifications_user_created ON notifications(user_id, created_at DESC);
+CREATE INDEX idx_notifications_user_read ON notifications(user_id, read, created_at DESC);
+CREATE INDEX idx_notifications_device ON notifications(device_id, created_at DESC);
+
+CREATE TRIGGER update_notifications_updated_at
+    BEFORE UPDATE ON notifications
+    FOR EACH ROW
+    EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();
+
+CREATE TABLE push_tokens (

6. from typing import Optional
7. 
8. _pool: Optional[asyncpg.Pool] = None
9. 
10. class NoResetConnection(_ap_connection.Connection):
11.     # asyncpg docs: Connection.get_reset_query() is used for pool reset.
12.     # Returning an empty string makes Connection.reset() a no-op.
13.     def get_reset_query(self) -> str:
14.         return ""
15. 
16. async def get_pool() -> asyncpg.Pool:
17.     """Return the existing connection pool, creating it if needed."""
18.     global _pool
19.     if _pool is None:
20.         settings = get_settings()
21.         _pool = await asyncpg.create_pool(
22.             dsn=settings.postgres_connection_string,
23.             min_size=2,
24.             max_size=20,
25.             command_timeout=30,
26.             connection_class=NoResetConnection,  # Use the custom connection class
27.         )
28.         logger.info("✅ Connected to PostgreSQL database")
29.     return _pool
30. 
31. 
32. async def close_pool() -> None:
33.     """Gracefully close the connection pool."""
34.     global _pool
35.     if _pool is not None:
36.         await _pool.close()
37.         _pool = None
38.         logger.info("PostgreSQL connection pool closed")

20.         direct_client.close()

40. def _install_workos_compatibility_shims(client: WorkOSClient) -> None:
41.     user_management = client.user_management
42. 
43.     if hasattr(user_management, "get_jwks_url"):
44.         return
45. 
46.     def _get_jwks_url() -> str:
47.         api_client = getattr(user_management, "_client", None)
48.         client_id = getattr(api_client, "client_id", None) or getattr(
49.             client, "client_id", None
50.         )
51.         if not client_id:
52.             raise RuntimeError("WorkOS client ID is required to build the JWKS URL")
53. 
54.         base_url = str(
55.             getattr(api_client, "base_url", None)
56.             or getattr(api_client, "_base_url", None)
57.             or "https://api.workos.com/"
58.         )
59.         return urljoin(base_url, f"sso/jwks/{client_id}")
60. 
61.     setattr(user_management, "get_jwks_url", _get_jwks_url)

64. def _get_compatible_workos_client(config: AuthConfig) -> WorkOSClient:
65.     cached_client = deploy_box_client._clients.get(config.workos_client_id)
66.     if cached_client is not None:
67.         return cached_client
68. 
69.     if not config.workos_api_key:

72.         )

36. ):

28. function formatRelativeTime(iso: string): string {
29.     const diff = Date.now() - new Date(iso).getTime();
30.     const minutes = Math.floor(diff / 60_000);
31.     if (minutes < 1) return 'Just now';
32.     if (minutes < 60) return `${minutes}m ago`;
33.     const hours = Math.floor(minutes / 60);
34.     if (hours < 24) return `${hours}h ago`;
35.     return `${Math.floor(hours / 24)}d ago`;
36. }
37. 
38. function formatLastSeen(iso: string | null): string {
39.     if (!iso) {
40.         return 'Last seen never';
41.     }
42. 
43.     const date = new Date(iso);
44.     if (Number.isNaN(date.getTime())) {
45.         return 'Last seen unknown';
46.     }
47. 
48.     return `Last seen ${formatRelativeTime(iso)}`;
49. }

11. function formatDate(iso: string): string {
12.     const d = new Date(iso);
13.     return d.toLocaleDateString(undefined, {
14.         weekday: 'long',
15.         year: 'numeric',
16.         month: 'long',
17.         day: 'numeric',
18.     }) + ' at ' + d.toLocaleTimeString(undefined, {
19.         hour: 'numeric',
20.         minute: '2-digit',
21.     });
22. }
23. 
24. function formatEventTitle(event: DeviceEvent): string {
25.     switch (event.event_type) {
26.         case 'assistance_requested':
27.             return 'Assistance requested';
28.         case 'assistance_acknowledged':
29.             return 'Request acknowledged';
30.         case 'assistance_resolved':
31.             return 'Request resolved';
32.         case 'pilot_seeded':
33.             return 'Pilot sign created';
34.         default:
35.             return event.event_type.replace(/_/g, ' ');
36.     }
37. }
38. 
39. function formatEventBody(event: DeviceEvent): string {
40.     const message = typeof event.payload?.message === 'string' ? event.payload.message : null;
41.     if (message) return message;
42. 
43.     const previousStatus = typeof event.payload?.previous_status === 'string'
44.         ? event.payload.previous_status
45.         : null;
46.     const newStatus = typeof event.payload?.new_status === 'string'
47.         ? event.payload.new_status
48.         : null;
49.     const confidence = typeof event.payload?.confidence === 'number'
50.         ? `${Math.round(event.payload.confidence * 100)}% confidence`
51.         : null;
52. 
53.     const parts = [
54.         previousStatus && newStatus ? `${previousStatus} -> ${newStatus}` : newStatus,
55.         confidence,
56.     ].filter(Boolean);
57. 
58.     if (parts.length > 0) {
59.         return parts.join(' • ');
60.     }
61. 
62.     return 'Recorded device event for the pilot sign.';
63. }
64. 
65. export default function NotificationDetailScreen() {
66.     const route = useRoute<RouteProp<RootStackParamList, 'NotificationDetail'>>();
67.     const { event } = route.params;
68. 
69.     return (
70.         <ScrollView style={s.container} contentContainerStyle={s.content}>
71.             <View style={s.header}>
72.                 <Text style={s.title}>{formatEventTitle(event)}</Text>
73.                 <Text style={s.date}>{formatDate(event.created_at)}</Text>
74.             </View>
75. 
76.             <View style={s.bodyCard}>
77.                 <Text style={s.body}>{formatEventBody(event)}</Text>
78.             </View>
79. 
80.             <View style={s.meta}>
81.                 <View style={s.metaRow}>
82.                     <Text style={s.metaLabel}>Event type</Text>
83.                     <Text style={s.metaValue}>{event.event_type}</Text>
84.                 </View>
85.                 {'new_status' in event.payload || 'previous_status' in event.payload ? (
86.                     <View style={[s.metaRow, s.metaRowSpaced]}>
87.                         <Text style={s.metaLabel}>Transition</Text>
88.                         <Text style={s.metaValue}>
89.                             {typeof event.payload.previous_status === 'string' ? event.payload.previous_status : 'unknown'}
90.                             {' -> '}
91.                             {typeof event.payload.new_status === 'string' ? event.payload.new_status : 'unknown'}
92.                         </Text>
93.                     </View>
94.                 ) : null}
95.             </View>

12. function formatDate(iso: string): string {
13.     const d = new Date(iso);
14.     return d.toLocaleDateString(undefined, {
15.         weekday: 'long',
16.         year: 'numeric',
17.         month: 'long',
18.         day: 'numeric',
19.     }) + ' at ' + d.toLocaleTimeString(undefined, {
20.         hour: 'numeric',
21.         minute: '2-digit',
22.     });
23. }
24.

25. const POLL_INTERVAL_MS = 30_000;
26. const HOME_SCREEN_REQUEST_TIMEOUT_MS = 10_000;

29. function formatRelativeTime(iso: string): string {
30.     const diff = Date.now() - new Date(iso).getTime();
31.     const minutes = Math.floor(diff / 60_000);
32.     if (minutes < 1) return 'Just now';
33.     if (minutes < 60) return `${minutes}m ago`;
34.     const hours = Math.floor(minutes / 60);
35.     if (hours < 24) return `${hours}h ago`;
36.     return `${Math.floor(hours / 24)}d ago`;
37. }
38. 
39. function formatLastSeen(iso: string | null): string {
40.     if (!iso) {
41.         return 'Last seen never';
42.     }
43. 
44.     const date = new Date(iso);
45.     if (Number.isNaN(date.getTime())) {
46.         return 'Last seen unknown';
47.     }
48. 
49.     return `Last seen ${formatRelativeTime(iso)}`;
50. }

11. function formatDate(iso: string): string {
12.     const d = new Date(iso);
13.     return d.toLocaleDateString(undefined, {
14.         weekday: 'long',
15.         year: 'numeric',
16.         month: 'long',
17.         day: 'numeric',
18.     }) + ' at ' + d.toLocaleTimeString(undefined, {
19.         hour: 'numeric',
20.         minute: '2-digit',
21.     });
22. }

👤 #177 User 29m 24s
What do I need to provde to make expo push registration/delivery work
💬 #178 Copilot 29m 37s

To make Expo push registration/delivery work here, I need four things:

  1. Expo app identity

    • Expo/EAS project ID

    • iOS bundle identifier

    • Android package name

    • Confirmation you’ll use a real device / development build, not just Expo Go

  2. Push credentials

    • iOS: APNs key/cert configured in Expo/EAS

    • Android: Firebase project + FCM server credentials configured in Expo/EAS

  3. Backend/runtime config

    • The API base URL the app should hit in real builds

    • Confirmation the backend should send through Expo Push API

    • If you want protected push sending, an Expo access token for server-side requests

  4. Product choices

    • Should push send for all opted-in operators or only the current signed-in device?

    • What title/body should assistance alerts use?

    • Should opening a push go to notification detail first or straight to the sign screen?

Practically, if you want me to finish the slice, provide:

  • EAS project ID

  • iOS bundle ID

  • Android package name

  • Whether APNs and FCM are already set up in Expo

  • Whether backend should use Expo Push API directly

  • The desired deep-link target on notification tap

39. function useQueryParam(name: string) {
40.     const url = Linking.useURL();
41. 
42.     return useMemo(() => {
43.         if (!url) return null;
44.         console.log('[DeepLink] Full URL:', url);
45.         const { queryParams } = Linking.parse(url);
46.         console.log('[DeepLink] Parsed queryParams:', queryParams);
47.         const v = queryParams?.[name];
48.         const result = typeof v === "string" ? v : (Array.isArray(v) ? v[0] : null);
49.         console.log(`[DeepLink] ${name} param:`, result);
50.         return result;
51.     }, [url, name]);
52. }

14. interface AuthState {

31. let lastExchangedCode: string | null = null;
32. let refreshInFlight: Promise<void> | null = null;

34. function getTokenExpiryMs(token: string | null): number | null {
35.     if (!token) return null;
36. 
37.     try {
38.         const [, payload] = token.split('.');
39.         if (!payload) return null;
40. 
41.         const normalized = payload.replace(/-/g, '+').replace(/_/g, '/');
42.         const padded = normalized.padEnd(Math.ceil(normalized.length / 4) * 4, '=');
43.         const decoded = JSON.parse(globalThis.atob(padded));
44.         return typeof decoded.exp === 'number' ? decoded.exp * 1000 : null;
45.     } catch (error) {
46.         console.warn('[Auth] Failed to decode token expiry:', error);
47.         return null;
48.     }
49. }
50. 
51. function isTokenFresh(token: string | null): boolean {
52.     const expiryMs = getTokenExpiryMs(token);
53.     if (!expiryMs) return false;
54.     return expiryMs - Date.now() > 60_000;
55. }

57. export const useAuthStore = create<AuthState>((set, get) => ({
58.     user: null,
59.     token: null,
60.     refreshToken: null,
61.     isAuthenticated: false,
62.     isLoading: true,
63.     sessionExpiredMessage: null,
64. 
65.     login: async () => {
66.         try {
67.             const redirectUri = getAuthRedirectUri();
68. 
69.             const response = await authAPI.initiateLogin(redirectUri);
70. 
71.             if (response.authorizationUrl) {
72.                 if (Platform.OS === 'web') {
73.                     window.location.href = response.authorizationUrl;
74.                 } else {
75.                     const result = await WebBrowser.openAuthSessionAsync(
76.                         response.authorizationUrl,
77.                         redirectUri,
78.                     );
79. 
80.                     if (result.type === 'success' && result.url) {
81.                         const parsed = ExpoLinking.parse(result.url);
82.                         const code = parsed.queryParams?.code as string | undefined;
83.                         if (code) {
84.                             await get().handleAuthCode(code);
85.                         }
86.                     }
87.                 }
88.             }
89.         } catch (error) {
90.             console.error('[Auth] Login error:', error);
91.         }
92.     },

94.     handleAuthCode: async (code: string) => {
95.         if (code === lastExchangedCode) {
96.             console.log('[Auth] Skipping duplicate code exchange');
97.             return;
98.         }
99.         lastExchangedCode = code;
100. 
101.         try {
102.             const authResponse = await authAPI.handleCallback(code);
103.             await get().setUser(authResponse.user, authResponse.accessToken, authResponse.refreshToken);
104.         } catch (error) {
105.             console.error('[Auth] Code exchange failed:', error);
106.             lastExchangedCode = null;
107.         }
108.     },
109. 
110.     setUser: async (user, token, refreshToken = null) => {
111.         try {
112.             if (user && token) {
113.                 await tokenStorage.setAccessToken(token);
114.                 if (refreshToken) {
115.                     await tokenStorage.setRefreshToken(refreshToken);
116.                 }
117.                 set({ user, token, refreshToken: refreshToken ?? null, isAuthenticated: true, isLoading: false });
118.             } else {
119.                 await tokenStorage.clear();
120.                 set({ user: null, token: null, refreshToken: null, isAuthenticated: false, isLoading: false });
121.             }
122.         } catch (error) {
123.             console.error('[Auth] Error saving auth state:', error);
124.             set({ isLoading: false });
125.         }
126.     },
127. 
128.     setTokens: async (token, refreshToken) => {
129.         try {
130.             await tokenStorage.setAccessToken(token);
131.             await tokenStorage.setRefreshToken(refreshToken);
132.             set({ token, refreshToken });
133.         } catch (error) {
134.             console.error('[Auth] Error saving tokens:', error);
135.         }
136.     },
137. 
138.     logout: async () => {
139.         let logoutUrl: string | undefined;
140.         try {
141.             const response = await authAPI.initiateLogout();
142.             logoutUrl = response.logoutUrl;
143.         } catch (error) {
144.             console.error('[Auth] Error calling logout API:', error);
145.         } finally {
146.             await tokenStorage.clear();
147.             set({ user: null, token: null, refreshToken: null, isAuthenticated: false });
148.         }
149. 
150.         if (logoutUrl) {
151.             if (Platform.OS === 'web') {
152.                 window.location.href = logoutUrl;
153.             } else {
154.                 await Linking.openURL(logoutUrl);
155.             }
156.         }
157.     },
158. 
159.     restoreSession: async () => {
160.         try {
161.             const timeoutMs = 8000;
162.             console.log('[Auth] restoreSession() called, timeout:', timeoutMs, 'ms');
163. 
164.             const restorePromise = (async () => {
165.                 console.log('[Auth] Step 1: Getting refresh token from storage...');
166.                 const t0 = Date.now();
167.                 const refreshToken = await tokenStorage.getRefreshToken();
168.                 console.log('[Auth] Step 1 done in', Date.now() - t0, 'ms. Has token:', !!refreshToken);
169. 
170.                 if (!refreshToken) {
171.                     console.log('[Auth] No refresh token — setting isLoading=false');
172.                     set({ isLoading: false });
173.                     return;
174.                 }
175. 
176.                 console.log('[Auth] Step 2: Refreshing token via API...');
177.                 const t1 = Date.now();
178.                 const tokens = await apiClient_refresh(refreshToken as string);
179.                 console.log('[Auth] Step 2 done in', Date.now() - t1, 'ms. Got new tokens:', !!tokens?.accessToken);
180. 
181.                 console.log('[Auth] Step 3: Saving new access token...');
182.                 await tokenStorage.setAccessToken(tokens.accessToken);
183.                 if (tokens.refreshToken) {
184.                     await tokenStorage.setRefreshToken(tokens.refreshToken);
185.                 }
186.                 set({
187.                     token: tokens.accessToken,
188.                     refreshToken: tokens.refreshToken ?? refreshToken,
189.                 });
190.                 console.log('[Auth] Step 3 done — tokens saved');
191. 
192.                 console.log('[Auth] Step 4: Fetching user profile...');
193.                 const t2 = Date.now();
194.                 const user = await authAPI.getCurrentUser();
195.                 console.log('[Auth] Step 4 done in', Date.now() - t2, 'ms. User:', user?.email || 'none');
196. 
197.                 set({ user, isAuthenticated: true, isLoading: false });
198.                 console.log('[Auth] Session restored successfully');
199.             })();
200. 
201.             const timeoutPromise = new Promise((_, reject) =>
202.                 setTimeout(() => reject(new Error('Session restore timed out')), timeoutMs)
203.             );
204. 
205.             await Promise.race([restorePromise, timeoutPromise]);
206.         } catch (error: any) {
207.             console.error('[Auth] Session restore FAILED:', error?.message || error);
208.             console.error('[Auth] Error name:', error?.name);
209.             console.error('[Auth] Error stack:', error?.stack?.substring(0, 300));
210.             if (error?.response) {
211.                 console.error('[Auth] HTTP status:', error.response.status);
212.                 console.error('[Auth] HTTP data:', JSON.stringify(error.response.data)?.substring(0, 200));
213.             }
214.             await tokenStorage.clear();
215.             set({ user: null, token: null, refreshToken: null, isAuthenticated: false, isLoading: false });
216.             console.log('[Auth] Cleared auth state after failure');
217.         }
218.     },
219. 
220.     ensureFreshSession: async () => {
221.         if (refreshInFlight) {
222.             await refreshInFlight;
223.             return;
224.         }
225. 
226.         const currentAccessToken = await tokenStorage.getAccessToken();
227.         if (isTokenFresh(currentAccessToken)) {
228.             return;
229.         }
230. 
231.         refreshInFlight = (async () => {
232.             const storedRefreshToken = await tokenStorage.getRefreshToken();
233.             if (!storedRefreshToken) {
234.                 get().handleSessionExpired();
235.                 throw new Error('No refresh token available');
236.             }
237. 
238.             const tokens = await apiClient_refresh(storedRefreshToken);
239.             await tokenStorage.setAccessToken(tokens.accessToken);
240.             if (tokens.refreshToken) {
241.                 await tokenStorage.setRefreshToken(tokens.refreshToken);
242.             }
243. 
244.             set((state) => ({
245.                 token: tokens.accessToken,
246.                 refreshToken: tokens.refreshToken ?? state.refreshToken ?? storedRefreshToken,
247.             }));
248.         })();
249. 
250.         try {
251.             await refreshInFlight;
252.         } catch (error) {
253.             console.error('[Auth] ensureFreshSession failed:', error);
254.             get().handleSessionExpired();
255.             throw error;
256.         } finally {
257.             refreshInFlight = null;
258.         }
259.     },
260. 
261.     handleSessionExpired: () => {
262.         tokenStorage.clear();
263.         set({
264.             user: null,
265.             token: null,
266.             refreshToken: null,
267.             isAuthenticated: false,
268.             isLoading: false,
269.             sessionExpiredMessage: 'Your session has expired. Please log in again.',
270.         });
271.     },
272. }));

274. /**
275.  * Direct axios call for token refresh — avoids going through the
276.  * intercepted apiClient, which would cause infinite loops.
277.  */
278. async function apiClient_refresh(refreshToken: string) {
279.     const API_URL = resolveApiV1BaseUrl();
280.     console.log('[Auth] apiClient_refresh — calling', `${API_URL}/auth/refresh`);
281.     try {
282.         const { data } = await axios.post(`${API_URL}/auth/refresh`, { refreshToken });
283.         console.log('[Auth] apiClient_refresh — success');
284.         return data as { accessToken: string; refreshToken: string };
285.     } catch (err: any) {
286.         console.error('[Auth] apiClient_refresh — FAILED:', err?.message);
287.         console.error('[Auth] apiClient_refresh — status:', err?.response?.status);
288.         throw err;
289.     }
290. }

💬 #210 Copilot 44m 59s

Expo push is wired for iOS. The app now registers an Expo push token after sign-in, unregisters it on logout, routes push taps to Home, and the backend sends assistance-request notifications through the Expo Push API.

What changed

  • Mobile: added Expo push registration/listeners in frontend_new\apps\mobile\App.tsx and src\lib\pushNotifications.ts

  • Auth/logout: clears/unregisters the stored Expo token in src\store\authStore.ts

  • Config: updated frontend_new\apps\mobile\app.json to use com.kalebwbishop.hazard-hero and added the expo-notifications plugin

  • Backend: added Expo delivery in backend\app\services\expo_push.py and hooked it into the existing assistance_requested flow in backend\app\routes\inference.py

What you still need to do outside the repo

  1. Run EAS credentials for iOS/APNs for this project.

  2. Build and install a development build or preview build on a physical iPhone.

  3. Sign in on the device and accept notification permissions.

  4. Trigger an assistance request and confirm the push arrives.

Notes

  • Push target is Home, as requested.

  • Android is still untouched.

  • EXPO_PUSH_ACCESS_TOKEN is supported on the backend but optional; Expo Push API will work without it.

👤 #211 User 46m 51s
What do you mean by run was credentials?
💬 #212 Copilot 46m 58s

I mean set up Apple push credentials in Expo/EAS for your iOS app so Expo can actually deliver APNs notifications.

For your app, that usually means running this from frontend_new\apps\mobile:

eas credentials

Then choose:

  1. iOS

  2. Your app/bundle ID: com.kalebwbishop.hazard-hero

  3. Let EAS manage push credentials / create or link the APNs key

You’ll likely need:

  • an Apple Developer account

  • to be logged into Expo/EAS

  • to authenticate with Apple when prompted

If you don’t have eas installed yet:

npm install -g eas-cli
eas login

In plain English: this step connects your iOS app in Apple’s system to Expo’s push service. Without it, the app can register an Expo push token, but pushes won’t reach the device.

👤 #213 User 48m 22s
Can I get arround C:\Users\KBishop\code\apps\smart-handicap-sign\frontend_new\apps\mobile>npx eas login ★ eas-cli@18.8.1 is now available. To upgrade, run: npm install -g eas-cli Proceeding with outdated version. request to https://api.expo.dev/graphql failed, reason: self-signed certificate in certificate chain Error: GraphQL request failed.
💬 #214 Copilot 48m 46s

Yes — usually by trusting your corporate/root CA, not by disabling TLS.

That error means Node/EAS doesn’t trust the certificate chain on your network. Best fix on Windows:

  1. Export your company proxy/root certificate as a .pem or .crt

  2. Point Node at it for this shell:

$env:NODE_EXTRA_CA_CERTS="C:\path\to\corp-root-ca.pem"
npx eas login

  1. If npm also has trouble, set its CA file too:

npm config set cafile "C:\path\to\corp-root-ca.pem"

Good ways to fix it

  • NODE_EXTRA_CA_CERTS for the current shell or user env

  • npm config set cafile ...

  • install the corporate root cert properly on the machine, then restart the terminal

Avoid if possible

$env:NODE_TLS_REJECT_UNAUTHORIZED="0"

That may bypass the error, but it disables TLS verification and is not a good long-term fix.

If you’re not sure where the cert is Ask your IT team for the corporate proxy/root CA certificate in PEM format.

Once that’s set, retry

npx eas login
npx eas credentials

💬 #218 Copilot 53m 8s

That just means the app is missing the EAS config file. Create frontend_new\apps\mobile\eas.json next to app.json.

Minimal starter file:

{
  "cli": {
    "version": ">= 18.8.1"
  },
  "build": {
    "development": {
      "developmentClient": true,
      "distribution": "internal"
    },
    "preview": {
      "distribution": "internal"
    },
    "production": {}
  }
}

Then rerun from:

C:\Users\KBishop\code\apps\smart-handicap-sign\frontend_new\apps\mobile

Commands:

npx eas login
npx eas credentials

If you want Expo to generate it for you instead, this also works:

npx eas build:configure

But with your certificate issue, manually creating eas.json is faster.
